msg:The exterior is magnificent, the area is excellent, the room is large, and the bed is wide. However, the interior is very old. There is an unusually strong smell of tobacco smoke when you enter the door. After opening the balcony door and ventilating for half an hour, the smell of tobacco becomes lighter, and the musty smell in the bathroom becomes prominent and lingering, accompanying the whole night, making people wonder if this is a big car inn on the national highway in the 1990s? Looking down, the obvious mildew and damage under the door frame and under the washbasin show that this is not an isolated case or a recent formation, but has been like this for a long time. Is it relying on a bottle of affordable Moutai that gives them the confidence to provide such facilities and services for a long time and never make improvements? I have used Ctrip.com to book hundreds of times over the years, and this is the first time I have made a bad review because I can no longer bear it. I give this virgin bad review to Moutai.
